function add_spot_on_map(obj_id, location_name, descr)
    if level.map_has_object_spot(obj_id,location_name)==0 then
        if descr==nil then
            descr=""
        end
        level.map_add_object_spot_ser(obj_id, location_name, descr)
    end
end
